mps	Te olo elaluyu, te gasagi yai tedali elaluali. Tama te megi te
mps	tǫde bidibo nai dabe augwali te sogo meni yai yai. Tama te be
mps	hulia saligo te genuai wę halua sai elalubadi, tama Godigo
mps	Mobo Bidi te daidu iba peyu, eda asu yai.

mps	kibisa nogode silama, tama nogo a naga olama, me badu nogo si
mps	wali tede aga olo bidai dao.

mps	mesegelisiąma, te bolu olo elaluali. Tama augwali sigo te ni
mps	kaya yabe dabe hobolama, tama augwa si te ugwa tiwai ilama,
mps	Tama tibaso, nago nai te tǫde bulubaso da, te nai bugagia me
mps	hologobeo. Te nago page bulu mu meniama, tama nage te tǫ sibi
mps	usu nama, te bulu wau bilibo bidi tiwai bidaibao,” te po wai.
mps	Tama tiyu, tama Mahalalel te kibu be 895 bidama, te aga isai dao.
mps	Te eno te tǫde wę asobo genuai mu pedalumainu elama, te
mps	tigidali bidibo ula elalubo nai dabe dola silimainu yaibao. Te
mps	tǫde tigidali nai dabe isila silaibao.
mps	tama wę aiyaba kekasa dulali. Te aiyaba dulubo sę idubadi,
mps	te tama polua nogo a naga, te 150 sogo teba usu nani.

mps	augwaligo te sela wabo te be haluabo nai te tamu ąįde
mps	elalubo hasa nogi sikau waligo nigai. Te si haluali madi ugwadu
mps	Tama te ni tolaluali ring dabe te tebol tolobo nai augwaligo te
mps	sesegede pąde ugwadu daiba muai.
mps	Augwaligo te gasa wiegi yai ugwa tigidali naga te obode walabo
mps	Tama augwaligo te sen gol deli deligo sabi te ring sigo kęnai
mps	Tama te bras altaba te wel geliyu, tama te sę yabo nai
mps	tigidaliba tiyu, tama te alta me te Genuai Bidigo nai naga dao
mps	homu eyu, tedali gasagi yai nai elalumainao.
mps	Tama Genuai Bidigo Mosesbolo ma walama, te Israel dabebolo e
mps	tiwai po walao po wali, “‘Te bidi me deligo te isiba
mps	tigidali ulama dabo ofa ebo bulmakau sesebaso da, teda agai te
mps	bulmakau omai wiegi yai mu sao, te aga tigide keni keni pobolo
mps	meni yai sesao. Te bidigo homugo te Genuai Bidigo agaba bugai
mps	haliga emaina homu eyu da, teda agai te tiwai ofa tama yao. Agai
mps	te Godigo Ugwa Be sunumi badu te bulmakau selasa aselama,
mps	tama te si wabo kibu homu dali te ili me te polalubo dini homu
mps	te wiegi yai me badu sao. Agai te namba wan homu me te namba tu
mps	homu si dali te sobadi yao.
mps	Tama agai te kau kibu kaneme meba te me si me si wali kom
mps	gąų te alta wiegi yai denami hano holobo te Genuai Bidigo
mps	gedu badu mubaso, usu yaibao. Te kau kibu kaneme tigidali me
mps	badu elalubadi ebaso da, agai te Ugwa Be sunumi bulu badu te
mps	augwaligo ofa ulubo badu sela solama, te alta aiyadu dogwali
mps	Genuai Bidigo Mosesbolo waliyu, te Israel dabeba te tiwai po
mps	Te pris nogi elalusąbo bidigo, ma te magi nai me deligo te ofa
mps	ebo kibude diąbaso da, teda te nai me ma te bidi te eno nai mu
mps	tama pedalumainu elama, te habu selalumainao. Te kibu kaneme te
mps	name ugwa me deliba tulalubaso da, dagego te name ugwa eno Ugwa
mps	Be obo tomode ąį telayao,” wali.
mps	Bidigo ma wego te dąų wali bomai po bolobaso da, teda aga te
mps	Genuai Bidigo hani tomode munu me bidigobeo,” wali.
mps	20-21 Agai te kaneme sąsągą bila silibo si da, teda agai
mps	te sipsip kibu sikilama, te haliga bono dabe me, te kibu sipsip
mps	sągą si me ąį telawali. Te nosali agai te kibu tobolu me
mps	ili me te sipsip kibu delage tigidali selama, te altaba munama,
mps	te tigidali siaba ulama, te keli naga elalueibao. Agai te Genuai
mps	Bidigo po wali gilama yali. Te siago tigidali dabo ofa ebo
mps	sipsip te sipsip ofa ebaso, te Genuai Bidigo te denami odama, te
mps	bugai haliga eyu yai dao.
mps	16-17 Te we bidi augwaligo te isiba tigidali ulabo ofa yainu
mps	sesali kibu si dabede te me deli agai sali, te ofago bomai pode
mps	wali po tiwai gilama, te augwaligo tigidali sogo kigamude ofa
mps	eyu yai. Tama agai te plaua selama, te wit ulubo ofa yali. Agai
mps	te dwasianu plaua nogogo selama, te plaua te isigo dela silibo
mps	4-6 Tiali goli dagego te kamel kibu, me rabit, me te masigi
mps	gabalode bidibo bolo gesia, te me tulamuo. Te hasa dabego te
mps	kaugo nosai tubo tiwai ebo dao, tiali goli augwaligo nogo
mps	sągą te age si elalubeo. Tama tiyu, dagego homugo augwali te
mps	eno gedude wiegi yai meni da homu elama, te dagego habu sao.
mps	“Ena Genuai Bidi, ena duga God dao. Tama tiyu, te duga digi
mps	dage enabolo mayu, te dolo isąbo kolesaga tagaluyu, te doloba
mps	pai kolesaga wali peyu, te meda meni yai wiegi yai tedali mu
mps	bidao. Magi baso meni, ena digi ena te magi meda meni yai wiegi
mps	yai tedali bidiyu, eno te wiegi yai kolesaga me doloba pai sę
mps	mu ebo dao. Tama te tǫde bilalubo dwasianu hasa dabe me
mps	tugimio. Tiyu, dage eno gedude meda pedelabuo.
mps	“Tama prisgo te bidi dili keni yali pesage bugagia suao. Te
mps	keni dwasianu tomoba pelama, te badu tigi nisi te tedela pedelai
mps	baso da, teda prisgo te bidibolo te tiwai po walao, ‘Nage God
mps	gedude wiegi yai ebeo.’ Te gasi te dili keni pedela sali
mps	pesagede pedelali da, te dwai nai mu dao.
mps	Tama prisgo te ugwa isiba ulao. Te oiyabe pedalubo tiwai yali
mps	nai, te isiba ulama, mu siago dela silimainao,” wali.
mps	“Tialima, prisgo te sipsip me oliv wel saibao, te nogogo
mps	tulama, te eno gedude iba eda yao.
mps	Te bomai pogo te dagebolo ola mayu, te mena nai te meda yai nai,
mps	ma te mena nai te wiegi yai eno gedude pedalubo, te bomai pogo
mps	page ola mabo po dao,” te po wai dao.
mps	Tama te we tigide poluago elibo gasi ebo po me, te bidi ma we
mps	tigide te aga naide tedela kaneme pedalubaso, te bidigo aga we
mps	dali pibo po te me te meda elalubao po wai dao.
mps	Te nosali agai te sęgę sela sąbo ofa ebaso da, teda te

mps	alta me, te pris dabe me, te Israel we bidi tigidali, te eno
mps	gedude wiegi yai ma pedalumainogo yaibao,” te po wai dao.
mps	Nago te naga aya sabi bidigo we dali penani sę me elamuo, magi
mps	baso meni, te we te nago ida sabi we elalubao. Te naga aga dali
mps	pibaso da, teda nago te nago aya sabi bidi hale dwai mu ilibo
mps	“Dagego te olo degai we bidi augwaliba te po dwai me wagio,
mps	‘Godigo dage dolabo sę elalubao.’ Dagego te gedu widai
mps	bage habela muabo bono gaga te sunumide me mugio. Dage ena
mps	Godide wi yao, duga Genuai Bidi dao,” wali.
mps	Dagego eno bomai po tigidali wali pao, magi baso meni, ena
mps	Genuai Bidigo dage eno we bidi wiegi yai pedalumainu sa muai
mps	Tama aga te eno Ugwa Be tagalama, te bidi tigi munalubo beba
mps	pelamuo. Agai tama sę eyu da, agai eno sel Ugwa Be meda
mps	pedalubo sę ilaibao. Dagego aga wel pilali, te eno dagebolo
mps	mani welgo te aga hetpris pedalumainu sa muai dao, tama tialima
mps	aga te isai bidi tigi munalubo beba pigio. Ena Genuai Bidigo eno
mps	Bugagia odao. Te dagego kibu tigi dwasianu dwai gana yaigo ofa
mps	ebaso da, teda eno godolo me egobeo.
mps	Te dagego gasa nai te bret dali ofa yao. Dagego te kibu sipsip
mps	wai te kibu be deli yai a naga me si ofa yao, te ogwa bidi
mps	bulmakau me deli, te omai sipsip si sobadi te ofa yao. Dagego te
mps	kenigo aga tigi dolali kibu me sigio. Te wiegi yai kibu naga
mps	sao. Te dagego enaba te isiba tigidali domainu ulubo ofa tiwai
mps	yao, te wit me wain meba te ofa dali muao, te dagego tigidali
mps	sogo ebo tiwai yao. Te ofago wiegi yai denami ebaso, ena Genuai
mps	Bidigo, eno godolo mu ebo dao.
mps	Genuai Bidigo Mosesbolo te po ma weyu, te tiwai wali, “Nago te
mps	sęgę 12 kilogram elalubo wiegi yai plaua selama, te plauago
mps	12 bret nigao. Te sęgę deli deli dobolama, te bret deli deli
mps	14-15 Te gasa bidi dagego tǫ abelemainogo mabo sogo, dagego
mps	koneao, te nisu naga kibu bede te nai tigidali wei ma mabo, te
mps	nisu naga sogo agai te bulali nai tau yali sabo me elalubo. Agai
mps	bugagia abelemainao, te tǫde mone usu nama dolo sao.

mps	bulu badu olo bidibo bagego lotu po mena tama wabowe’ wabo.
mps	‘Teda dago me te tobage kolesaga elama, lotu po waina,’ te
mps	12-18 Tiali goli, dagego te tigidali hani genuai me dwasianu
mps	kemodage, me hulide bilibo uni, me kugidi, me te toli, me te

mps	augwaligo hupou nogi wabo, me te pato, me augwaligo komoran

mps	isilao. Ma, bidi deligo naga suai baso da, teda te we o bidi
mps	elama isilabo sunumi meni yaibao. Usugobeo.

mps	nigaibao. Tama eno po agabolo mayu yaibao. Tama eno po me deli

mps	boide isai digi, gasa bidigo augwaligo te we sabuo,’ te ofisa

mps	yali dao. Tama te wegigo te bidi dabego aga tau somainogo hae

mps	te we sela sąwai dao. Ma, te wego nosali pali te bidi isibaso
mps	Dolo tama mao. Tama tiyu da, dage e tǫde bobobage sogo bugagia
mps	bidaibao, te Genuai Bidi dago God agai dabolo mawainogo ebo te

mps	tagala palaibao, te tulubage side naga. Tama agai dagego

mps	negeli emainogo me egobeo.

mps	nai dabe wi selama, tama augwaligo tibo sę elama, tama

mps	bagulagasao wai. Tama augwaligo te Josua pobeasa soabo sę eyu,

mps	wali. “Magi baso, eno homugo ena polo pelama, tama te profet
mps	bidi sugi paio, tama ena ma polo asaibao,” wali.
mps	Israel kingo te Siria king agai te pas sulama, tama agai te aga
mps	holobo ugwa pisą yali. Aga te ugwa pisą yali te aga haligade
mps	sębę dwai mu ebo page ola mayu, tama tiwai. Tama agai e
mps	tiwai po tama wai, “Magi elama, te Siria king bidigo te po
mps	enabolo tolali, eno menagi elama, e bidi oiyabe gasi dodolomainu
mps	waliwe? Agai homugo ena God da weyu, tama te bidi dabe bugagia
mps	bidibo me, ma te bidi isibo me, te bomo agai homugo eno
mps	elalubawe weyu, waliwe, a? Eno koneanio, agai homugo ena dali
mps	boi hwįainu tų gegeyu walio, te tama dao,” wali.
mps	Tama Elisa, te Godigo profetgo, e tiwai po tama hanalu wali,
mps	“Te hwą menade tula paliwe?” Tama profetgo te Elisabolo te
mps	hwą tula pali pesage ola mani. Awe, tama Elisago ni nologo
mps	dwasianu toga selama, tama te węba sąyani, tama te hwą
mps	wędu aiyadu edaba pedalu gulama, ąį daide pilali.
mps	Tama te king tonaluyu tau sabo gavman ofisa bidi me deli aga te
mps	king dali asali. Te bidigo te Elisago wali po odali, awe, tama
mps	agai te po wei e tama ponani, “Tagalao. Tialima, Genuai Bidi
mps	God aga digi te dagalude elalubo moni bakstua tų dalama, te
mps	umabo nai daba gealugi sogo da, teda eno homugo dago e tiwai
mps	dwasianu monego dago nai abelebo me usu egi menigi da,” wali.
mps	Tama te Hasaelgo agabolo hanalu wali, “Genuai bidi, magi baso
mps	Tama te Jesebel isibo si, te agai tigi selasa pelama, pubaligi
mps	pabo bidi menia saibao. Mu meni. Tama agai tigi te yowi dabego
mps	tueibao, te Jesril hanu pąde.’ Genuai Bidigo te po wai.”
mps	Te profet bidigo te Genuai Bidigo po Jehubolo pusa silama, tama
mps	aga te be tų dala sąnama, tama aga wi pai.
mps	Tama augwali ma begasa pelama, te Jehubolo te sę yali po
mps	pusugi pali, tama agai e tama po pusali, “Te sę te Genuai
mps	Bidi God aga sę ebo bidigo pedauwalidu wali podu dolo mu
mps	pedalali, te Elaija aga te Tisbe hanude bidali bidi dao. Genuai
mps	Bidigo e tama po wai dao, ‘Te kwin we Jesebel isibo sogo, te
mps	yowigo agai tigi tueibao,’ wali, ‘te Jesril hanu tǫde
mps	Tama augwaligo te tibo god Bal noma nigali piksa me, te lotu po
mps	wabo be me, te augwaligo mu dolali, tama augwaligo te lotu be te
mps	di be mu nigilali, tama te be me tama elalu, bidada asama, megi
mps	e po asębo bidi dabe bidali sogoba usu nagasalio.
mps	tama pris bidi dabego te we bidi dabe augwaligo dagebolo mabo
mps	mone dagego bugagia tonaluao. Tama te sogo dagego suali madigi,
mps	te Genuai Bidigo tempel be te me badu pedai badu deli dolai baso
mps	da, teda dagego te mone selama, tama dagego te tempel be dolali
mps	dodolobo bidi abelao,” wali.
mps	Tama Elisago kingbolo e tama po wali, “Megi nago te dwasianu
mps	windo tų nage pelama, dagi pelama, tama nago te giliga asoboba
mps	tonaluao.” Tama tialima, te king Jehoasgo te enesigi balibi
mps	petegelama, tama pelama, aga pelama, te dwasianu windo tų dagi
mps	pali. Tama Elisago te kingbolo te po wali, “Tama nago enesigi
mps	balibi dolama, tama te pelama ene enigi pao.” Tama te king
mps	Jehoasgo agai wali po selama, tama tiali, tama Elisago i wali,
mps	“Te ene, te Genuai Bidigo ene dao. Te enego te Siria hani
mps	aiyaba elaluaibao. Tama tialima, te sogo te nago Siria hani dali
mps	boi hwįbo sogo, te augwa te Afek taunde boi hwįaibao, tama
mps	nago augwali mu silaibao,” wali.
mps	Tama nosali me badu sogo te aga tudi badu te king bidi nigilali,
mps	tama agai boi hwįgi pelama, tama te Elat taun te boi bidi
mps	dabego nogode elalubadi ma sali. Tama te taun te me badu pedai
mps	badu dolali, te agai me dodolali.
mps	Tama te king Pekahia agai boi hwįbo ami gavman tobolu bidi me
mps	deli, te bidi agai nogi Peka, te bidi aga aya Remaliago ogwa da,
mps	tama te bidi Peka dali, te me badu bidi dabe te moni taun Gileat
mps	bulu bidigo te 50 bidi dabe dali, augwali sisinama, tama
mps	augwaligo te king Pekahia ela muabo po minama, dąų wali. Te
mps	king Pekahia aga te Samaria bulude te king be te bomai daga rum
mps	habude bidibadi yaide, tama te bidi dabe augwali te bomai rum
mps	habu tomoba pelama, tama augwaligo te king Pekahia ela muani.
mps	Tama augwaligo te bidi me si nogi Argop me te Arie, te bidi si
mps	me ela muani. Tama te ami tobolu bidi Pekago te king bidi
mps	Tama te Genuai Bidigo tempel be togobe badu pąde tama, te king
mps	aga dulabo dwasianu be gagawai nai me deli elaluai, augwaligo te
mps	nai nigali page e tiwai, te giliga asobo badu paliainu, te Sabat
mps	side te madi tiwai nigai nai da, tama megi Ahasgo po obaso,
mps	augwaligo te nai hųgiali. Tama augwali te Genuai Bidigo tempel
mps	be obo banis tųba te king pabo tųba te augwali pai, tama
mps	augwaligo te tųde te dwagi yai au yai nai elaluali me
mps	hųgiali, tama te au yai nai te bidi dabego munu me subeo. Tama
mps	te king Ahasgo agai te Asiria kingo homu wali painu homu yai,
mps	tama agai te tobage sę te tempel bede sę yali.
mps	Tiali goli, te hani dabe deli deli augwaligo te tibo god noma
mps	nigilama, teba wali pabo kolesaga me idu bidali. Tama augwaligo
mps	te god noma nigali, te polobadu te Israel hani dabego te lotu po
mps	wali pesagede muna muna pai, te bulu du dabede. Tama augwaligo
mps	te deli deli hani augwa god deli deli nidigi pelama, tama augwa
mps	bidibo taun bulude muna muna pali.
mps	Nago homugo olo po tama wabogo bomo eyu, te wabao, te boi
mps	hwįbo da nago aiyaba me elaluaibawe, a? Nago ena dali hagoma
mps	ebawe? Naga homugo dego asama, nage tau sagasabo weyu, tama nago
mps	Te king Hesekiago agai te king Senakeripgo tolali pas agai te
mps	bidi dabego nogode agai sali. Agai te pas asęani po neda
mps	silama, tama agai te Genuai Bidigo tempel be tomoba selasa pali.
mps	Tama agai te pas te Genuai Bidi bidibo pesage pąde muani, tama
mps	agai pisaganama, tama bugagia dodolama, muani.
mps	Tialima, hasia bolo king Hesekiago Aisaiabolo e tama po hanalu
mps	wali, “Genuai Bidigo agai enabolo mena tama tiwai sę ola
mps	menama, tama tedu eno koneaibao, eno ma wiegi yai pedalama, tama
mps	duba ena nago gedude te tempel beba paibawe?” te po hanalu
mps	Tama te king Manase isali, tama augwaligo te aga te kingo be
mps	sesegede te obo tomode te tǫ me deli elalubo madigi te king
mps	Manase pubulali. Te tǫ te augwaligo e tama nogi wabo, te tǫ
mps	te Usago tǫ da. Te aga ogwa, agai nogi te e dao, Emon, tama te
mps	bidi agai te bidigo sę yali silide te aga king sę yali.
mps	Te king aga te Genuai Bidigo be mabo dolo elalubo bobobage pos
mps	dolalubo madigi aga dolaluali, tama agai te Genuai Bidi dali e
mps	tama bomai po dąų wali. Agai te tigidali te bomai po te buku
mps	tomode muani po wali paibao wai. Agai te po bodolu selama polali
mps	deli homu naga, deli kolesaga naga tigidali bomai po me, me te
mps	Genuai Bidi agai po me wali mu paibao. Tama te tigidali we bidi
mps	dabego me augwali tigidaligo te bodolu selama, dąų wali po
mps	delidu naga wali paibao olama, polali.
mps	Tama te king Nekogo agai te bidi Eliakim sali, te king Josaiago
mps	gasa ogwa me da, tama te king Neko agai homugo te bidi Eliakim
mps	aga te Juda hanigo king bidi nigilainu yali, te bidigo te aga
mps	aya Josaiago king sę yali silide bidiyu, king sę yali. Tama
mps	te king Neko agai te bidi Eliakim nogi hasegelama, tama aga nogi
mps	Jehoiakim poali. Tama nosali te king Nekogo te Joahas aga te
mps	Isip buluba odasa pelama, tama aga te Isip bulude bididubadi
mps	yaide, isibo bodoluba usu nigi pali.
mps	Te Babilon king bidi Nebukatnesar aga te Babilonde king bidi
mps	bidibadi, agai kibu be te bidi sese deli pąde, te 19 yia, aga
mps	king bidi bidama, tama te nogo a wabo poluago dei te nogo a
mps	olama, te me badu nogogo si, te 7 dei, megi e kibu be tomode
mps	tama, te king Nebukatnesar te Babilon king bidigo aga sę ebo
mps	gavman ofisa bidi me deli, aga te Jerusalem buluba asali. Te
mps	bidi Nebusaradan agai te king tonalubo ami soldia bidi dabe
mps	tonalubo tobolu bidi dao.
mps	Te Kusgo ogwa dabego nogi e tiwai, Seba, me Havila, me Sapta, me
mps	Rama, me Sapteka. Ramago ogwa si ame nai, Seba me Dedan dao.
mps	Sobalgo ogwa dabe nogi e tiwai, Alvan, me Manahat, me Ebal, me
mps	Sefi, me Onam dao. Sibeongo ogwa dabe nogi e tama, Aia me Ana
mps	Tama Abigel te Ismael hani bidi Jetergo selama, tama Abigelgo
mps	ogwa deli ame nani, aga nogi Amasa dao.
mps	Te Kalepgo gasa si wali we hani me, te Maka dao. Te Makago ogwa
mps	dabe nogi e tiwai, Seber, me Tirhana,
mps	Judago ogwa hani meba nogi e tiwai elalubao, Peres, me Hesron,
mps	me Karmi, me Hur, me Sobal dao.
mps	Te tobolu bidi dabego ame nani ogwago bulali wai dabe hani te
mps	umabo genuai mu pedelama,
mps	Tama tialima, Israelgo Godigo te Asiria king bidi Pul homu
mps	hodolali, te aga gasa nogi me Tiklat Pileser wali. Tama te
mps	Asiria dabego te Israel dabeba boi hwįagaselama, te augwali
mps	aiyaba elalualio. Tama te Asiria dabego augwali selama, te Hala
mps	tǫba kalabus mugi pali, te Habor tǫba me, te wę Gosan
mps	pąde te Hara bulu du pesageba pali. Tama augwali tede
mps	bidalubadi, te e buku asęani bidi bidali sogoba usu nai dao.
mps	Te ede nogi elalubo bidi dabe te king Devitgo te Genuai Bidigo
mps	bede wiegi yai po wabo nai musik elabo bidi dabe sa muai dao. Te
mps	Dąų Wali Bomo Yai Po Muani Halobage te Genuai Bidigo sel
mps	ugwa beba muagaselama nosali badu Devitgo te hani dąį ilai
mps	Tama augwaligo te nogo si olama sela taun dabe te Gersongo
mps	haniba dąį ilama mawai. Te taun dabe te Isakar, me Aser, me
mps	Naptali, me te Manase hani pedai te Basan tǫde bidali, te hani
mps	me si me sigo taun dabe manio.
mps	Te Naptaligo ogwa dabe nogi e tama da, Jasiel, Guni, Jeser, me
mps	Salum da. Te wai dabe augwa auwa mosi te Bilha da, te Jekopgo si
mps	me Abisua, me Naman, me Ahoa,
mps	Te Benjamingo hanide tobolu bidi me deli nogi Salu, te Mesulamgo
mps	ogwa. Mesulam te Hodaviago ogwa da, tama Hodavia te Hasenuago
mps	Miklot te Simeamgo aya. Te augwali hani dabe te Benjamingo gasa
mps	hani te Jerusalem pąde bidali te hani dabe pąde bidalio.
mps	Te Devitgo bomai ami bidi dabego nogi da e tiwai, Jasobeam te
mps	Hakmoni hani, aga te polalubo ofisa bidi. Me sogo deli sogo
mps	Jasobeamgo aga hwįbo sesemone ene tolalu, te 300 boi bidi dali
mps	hwįnama, te tigidali ela silai dao.
mps	te Adina te Sisago ogwa, aga te Ruben hanide tobolu bidi me deli
mps	da, tama te Adina hani te bidi sese deli nogo si 30 bidi da,
mps	Te Livai hanigo ami bidi sese umabo te 4,600 ami bidi elaluai.
mps	Te agai ogwa dabe nogi e tama da, Samua, me Sobap, me Natan, me
mps	Augwaligo te bidi Kenaia dąį ilama te halobage sela asobo
mps	sę tigidali tonaluali, magi baso meni, agai te tobage sę ebo
mps	mu koneai bidi. Kenaiago te tobage sę sesemane sogo tonalubo
mps	Augwali te gasa hani dabego tǫde subigila bilalualio.
mps	Dage tigidali hani we bidi,
mps	te wiegi yai mu da, tama sesemane sogo
mps	Te kingo tama te eno be sęwaibao. Te eno agai hani bidide naga
mps	te sesemane sogo king pedalumainu yaibao po walio.
mps	Te Sadok dali Ahimelek si, augwali si pris bidali. Sadok te
mps	Ahitupgo ogwa. Te Ahimelek te Abiatargo ogwa. Tama Savsa te
mps	kingo sę ebo kuskus bidi bidai.
mps	Tialima Devitgo te Joapbolo te gasa ami ofisa dabeba te tiwai po
mps	walali, “Dage pelama, te Israel we bidi nedegi pao,” wali.
mps	“Dage te tǫ pedai tigidali badu bilao, te taun Berseba te
mps	saut badu usu nama pao, tama te taun Dan te not badu me pao.
mps	Tama dagego te sę yali po asęnama enaba sesao, tama tibaso
mps	eno te we bidi dabego namba koneaibao,” wali.
mps	Tama Devitgo te nil dabe nigabo ain umabo hauwa sisinani, tama
mps	te be sunumi dabe dąų walabo ain delage dabe me nigabo ain
mps	sisinani. Tama me, agai te bras hauwa mu sisinani, te bidigo aga
mps	sęgę dabe dagalabo usu meni yai dao.
mps	Gersongo gomunai ogwa te Sebuel dao.
mps	te namba 15 te Bilga hani, me te namba 16 te Imergo hani dąį
mps	Te namba 8 wagisu augwaligo te Jesaia dali, aga ogwa dabe me, te
mps	aga deli hani dabe dali dąį ilai dao.
mps	Tama satugo Supim me Hosa dąį ilama, te giliga dega sabo
mps	badu tonalumainogo yali, tama te sunumi nogi augwaligo Saleket
mps	te me tonaluao wali. Te sunumi Saleket te ugwaba holobo pabo
mps	tų pąde elaluali. Augwaligo te hani deli deligo te sę
mps	tonaluabo sogo dąį ilali, tama augwali te sunumi tonalubo
mps	sę me hasegelu me hani hasegelu iduai dao.
mps	Heldai te Netofa taun bidigo te bidi sese umabo 24,000 bidi
mps	augwali te 12 wagi soabo poluade te sę ebo bidi dabe
mps	tonalualio. Heldai te Otniel hani bidi dao.
mps	Tama me te nogi asęanide te tigidali nai te Godigo Mobo Noma
mps	Bidigo Devitba ola mani, te sisinabo pesage te Genuai Bidigo
mps	tempel be sę yabo pesage nigabo, me te piksa noma dabe elalubo
mps	ola mani te sisinibo pesage bagulali habu dabe, me te Godigo
mps	bede mone mubo be, me te Genuai Bidiba dąį ilama te bidi
mps	dabego mabo wiegi yai nai dabe ola mawai dao.
mps	Tama te side te we bidi dabe augwa te ąį dabe me kibu mi
mps	dabe tuali, te gasa ofa yali nai dabe tuyu, tama augwa wiegi yai
mps	pemene umabo mu te Genuai Bidiba yai.
mps	Tama eno genuai be mu sę yaibao. Magi baso meni. Dago Godigo
mps	genuai nogi mu elaluyu, tama me genuai bomo mu elaluyu, tama
mps	agai gasa meba god dabe edelama aiyaba elalubao.
mps	Tama te tank wę bogo badu tobolu badu augwaligo te lain si te
mps	kau kibu omai piksa noma tiwai si nigali. Te piksa noma sesego
mps	te tank wę ugwadu daide usu nama nigilama silalio. Tama te
mps	tigidali hap mita elalua pabo tomode te nogo si 10 kau kibu noma
mps	elalua pali. Tiali goli augwaligo te piksa noma nigilama te
mps	tankde daganebeo. Menio. Te augwaligo te tank nigali sogo
mps	augwaligo te piksa dali tama nigali. Tama augwali te tank pedai
mps	Te pris bidi dabe augwaligo te Dąų Wali Bomai Po Munalubo
mps	Halobage te Genuai Bidigo tempel be tomoba polo muani, tama
mps	augwali buluba ma teda soabo sogo da, te musik elebo bidi hanigo
mps	biugel bu weyu, te plet bras tama elebo gagalali. Tama augwaligo
mps	Genuai Bidigo nogi ugwaba sabo tęąbi po tama wali. Augwaligo
mps	tęąbi po e tama tiwai wali, “Dago Genuai Bidiba buba hwi
mps	po wainao. Magi baso meni. Aga da, te da dali wiegi yai kolesaga
mps	ebo bidi dao. Agai da godolo mu ebo kolesaga te gamonaibao,”
mps	wali. Te augwaligo tęąbi po wabo si, polo tama te genuai
mps	pǫgo te Genuai Bidigo tempel be pągąna sagasali.
mps	“Te tigidali we bidigo sęgę sabo sę ebo dao. Tama
mps	tialima, dago nage dali sęgę sabo sę eyu da, tama nago da
mps	dali wado elama, tama nago boi bidi dabego da dali
mps	hwįagaselama da aiyaba elaluama, tama da kalabus elama, da
mps	digibulu o pąde elalubo kantri dabeba pomainu sula tagaliyu,
mps	Te kantri Israelde te gasa bulu we bidi me bidali. Te augwali te
mps	Hit hani, me Amor hani, me Peres hani, me Hivi hani, me Jebus
mps	Te king Hiramgo boskru dabego Solomongo genuai sip te kantri
mps	Tarsisba sela peyu ebo dao. Te Solomongo te sip dabe tagala
mps	palobo sogo da, augwali kibu be sela mu biliyu ebo dao. Tama
mps	augwaligo gol dabe, me silva dabe, me elefan kibugo kele dabe,
mps	me haniani hasa monki dabe sela asiyu ebo dao. Tama nosali
mps	augwali ma biligi peyu ebo dao.
mps	“Nage king Rehoboam te Juda dabego king pageba, me Juda hani
mps	we bidi, me Benjamin hani we bidi pageba pelama, tama
mps	augwalibolo e tama po waligi pao.
mps	Genuai Bidigo king Rehoboamgo aga digi aga aiyaba elaluama tama
mps	aga dologode bidibo suali. Tama me agai meba wiegi yai kolesaga
mps	te kantri Judade elalubo suali. Tama tibaso, augwali dali aga
mps	sębę me ebeo, te Rehoboam dali, tama agai aga mu dolama
mps	Te Juda bulude tigidali taun dabede agai tigidali tibo godiba
mps	lotu wabo pesage sese sela sąnama, tama agai te wiegi yai
mps	denami hano holobo ofa ulabo te alta dabe me sese tama dolama
mps	tagalali. Agai te kantri bugagia tonalubadi te boi me pedalobeo
mps	“Eno homugo dadi si abagi si bidabo po dąų waibao, te
mps	polobadu dadi sigo aya sigo yali gilama. Tama tibaso eno te
mps	silva me gol dali si nagebolo te tolobao. Eno homugo nago te
mps	Israel dabego king Basa dali dąų wali po hųgia sąyao.
mps	Tama agai aga ami dabe sela peyu eno tǫ taga pomainao,”
mps	Tama kibu be meba pela silai madi, te Jehosafat aga taun
mps	Samariaba pali, te king Ahap suainogo. Tama tialima king Ahapgo
mps	aga hani sę bidi dabebolo walama, augwaligo sipsip kibu hauwa
mps	eliyu, me kau kibu eliyu elama, augwali genuai nai ulali, te
mps	king Jehosafat me aga dali asali hanigo tuabo nai. Magi baso
mps	meni. Ahapgo Jehosafatbolo agai taun Ramot te distrik Gileatba
mps	boi hwįgi pabo tau somainogo hanalu wainogo.
mps	Tiali goli te ami bidi dabe augwali hwįbo sę idubadi, te
mps	Siria ami bidi me deligo enesigi kegelama, tama Israel ami bidi
mps	dabe bidiboba uba ene subigila enani. Tama te enego Ahapgo tigi
mps	boi hwįbo ugwago aga tigi bugagia me dualisąma yali tede mu
mps	dolali. Tama aga karis guni tubo bidibolo e tama po walali,
mps	“Ena polo dolalio. Te karis polo begelama, tama hwįbo pesage
mps	Te king Jehosafat me te tigidali we bidi augwaligo te po odobo
mps	si, teda te we bidi sese augwali sese bogoli sugunama, tǫba
mps	tobolu basi guluama, tama Genuai Bidiba lotu po wali.
mps	Nago Israel dabego dwai kolesaga wali peyu, tama nago Juda dabe
mps	me Jerusalem dabe kegelama, tama augwaligo God tudiba mani dao.
mps	Nago Ahap aga hani dali augwaligo te Israel hani dali kolesaga
mps	tiwai mu tama te yali dao. Tama me ma, nago naga ama solo mu
mps	elama isilai dao. Augwali wiegi yai bidi dabe mu, tama augwaligo
mps	kolesaga nago kolesaga mu edelai dao.
mps	Te kwin Ataliago te we bidigo genuai po kulukulu wabo odali, te
mps	kingde wiegi yai homu iyu udula biliyu ugwa eda ebo po odali.
mps	Tama agai aga be tagalama, Genuai Bidigo tempel beba pali, te we
mps	King Joas aga ofisa dabe dali augwaligo te Sekaraiago wali po
mps	wei ebeo, tama augwaligo aga ela isilabo po miani. Tama tialima
mps	kingo pode te bidi dabego masigigo Sekaraia enani, tama aga te
mps	Genuai Bidigo tempel be bagulali obo tomode sisinibo pesagede
mps	Nosali Israel dabego king Jehoas aga isali, tama Juda dabego
mps	king Amasia aga 15 kibu be ma bidama, tama nosali augwaligo aga
mps	Tama nosali, Jotamgo aga ami bidi dabe dali augwali te Amon dabe
mps	king dali aga ami bidi dabe dali boi hwįgi pali. Tama Jotamgo
mps	ami bidi dabego Amon dabego ami bidi dabe aiyaba mu elaluali.
mps	Tialima Jotamgo Amon dabebolo agabolo takis mao po wali. Tama te
mps	kibu bede augwaligo agabolo te 3,400 kilogram silva mani, me
mps	1,000 ton sęgę wit, me 1,000 ton sęgę rais bali agabolo
mps	mani. Tama te deli tiwai takis te namba 2 kibu bede me namba 3
mps	Te Hesekia aga king bidali sogo te namba wan kibu bede te namba
mps	wan poluade, te kibu bede agai Genuai Bidigo tempel be sunumi ma
mps	dayali, tama agai bidi mebabolo te sunumi ma dodolao po wali.
mps	35-36 Te pris dabego iside mu dela silibo ofa hauwa mu yali.
mps	Tiali goli augwaligo te sę deli naga ebeo. Menio. Augwaligo
mps	homu deliba ebo ofa kibu ili me ulali, tama augwaligo te we
mps	bidigo te isigo mu dela silibo ofa dali ulabo wain me augwaligo
mps	sali, tama augwaligo ofa tiwai gelali. King Hesekia me te we
mps	bidi augwaligo Godigo augwali tau selama, te sę dabe polo
mps	silimainu yali kone palali. Tialima augwaligo Godiba wiegi yai
mps	homu pemene mu yali. Tama te kolesagago augwaligo te ofa ebo
mps	kolesaga me Genuai Bidigo tempel be tomode lotu wabo kolesaga ma
mps	Te we bidi dabe augwaligo te nai dabe sesidu geani, te namba 3
mps	poluadu gagalama, pelama, namba 7 poluaba usu nigi pali.
mps	Tama te king Senakeripgo pas dabe asęnama, Genuai Bidi God
mps	posobo po wali, te Israel dabego God Genuai Bidibolo. Te pas
mps	dabede e tama tiwai po dabe elaluali, “Te eno meba kantri dabe
mps	dali hwįani sogo, augwa god dabego augwali tau selama, tama
mps	augwaligo ena aiyaba me elaluai menio. Tama Hesekiago Godigo me
mps	dage aga we bidi me tau sogobeo. Mu menio,” tama po asęna
mps	Tama agai meba hanigo tibo god dabe sela sąyu, me aga digi
mps	Genuai Bidigo tempel be tomode muani te tibo god piksa dabe sela
mps	sąyani. Tama elalubo bulu dude te alta dabe sela sąyani.
mps	Tama meba te alta dabe te Jerusalemde elaluali dabe sese tama
mps	sela sąyani, tama agai te nai dabe taun buluba selasa pelama,
mps	“Te bomai po buku eno megi sali da, tede Genuai Bidigo homugo
mps	dago wali pomainu homu yali po e bukude haninama te wali dao.
mps	Tiali goli dago wąį nǫų dabego te po wali pai menio.
mps	Tama tialima, te tama tialigo da, Genuai Bidigo da dali sębę
mps	genuai mu emainu ilali dao. Tiali goli dago megi Genuai Bidigo
mps	te buku polo te sali dao. Tama tialima, eno homugo dage pelama,
mps	Genuai Bidibolo hanalugi pao, tama ena dali Israel bulude bidibo
mps	we bidi me Juda bulude bidibo we bidi, dago mena sę emainu
mps	egowe page sugi piąo,” king Josaiago te po wali.
mps	Augwaligo te nai te Josaia aga king bidibadi te kibu be 18
mps	Te hasia kibu be tede te bidi Sairus te Persia kantri tǫ
mps	pedaide king bidali sogo, God Genuai Bidigo aga homu hodolama,
mps	tama agai po me deli walio. Agai te po asęnama, tama agai te
mps	tonalubo tǫ pedai tigidaliba tolali. Tama te po sela pabo bidi
mps	dabe augwaligo te we bidi dabeba nedemainu yalio. Te sę
mps	pedelali, te Genuai Bidigo te polobadu bidali profet bidi
mps	Jeremaiabolo po menama, tama Jeremaiago te Israel dabeba pusali
mps	po me deli te poba usu nanio.
mps	E da te Juda dabego taun nogi hauwa dao. Te taun dabe te Juda
mps	tǫba ma pali bidi hani dabe augwa wąį dabego page bulu
mps	taun dao. Te Betlehem taun bidi dabego namba te 123 dao,
mps	Te bidi nogi me Baslut, Mehida, Harsa,
mps	Tama tialima, augwali pelama, te Serubabel me tobolu bidi dabe
mps	te Israel deli deli hani bage sugi pelama, tama augwaligo te po
mps	wai, “Da te dage dali te Godigo be sę yagasomainu ilao,”
mps	po wali. “Dago me te dagego Godiba lotu wabo dao,” po wali.
mps	“Tama te Asiria tǫ king bidi Esarhadongo da te e bulu tǫ
mps	pedaiba tagala palama bidagasali, te megi e sogoba usu
mps	nagasobao, dago te Godiba ofa ebo dao,” po wali.
mps	Tama dago te tobolu bidi dabe augwaligo nogi po me hanalu wali,
mps	te dego te sę tonalubo te dago koneama, te pas nageba tolainu
mps	te po me dago hanalu wai dao.
mps	8-9 Augwaligo te bulu Babilon te deli wabo polua, dei deli
mps	wabode, te taga soalio. Tama Godigo augwali tau sobaso, tama
mps	augwali te Jerusalemba te a naga polua, te 5 mun, dei deli, te
mps	sogo te Jerusalemba sabolali, magi baso meni, te digibulu mu pai
mps	Tama Elifelet, me Juel, me Semaia, te Adonikam hani bidi dao.
mps	Tama te bidi sese sela, te 60 hani bidi te bidi sela dali
mps	pepelawalio. Tiali goli, augwali te sogo da dali asobeo, augwali
mps	“Tiali goli megi da, God, dago Genuai Bidi, nago te olo tau
mps	mabo wiegi yai kolesaga te daba gagalama ma yalio. Tama da
mps	dwasianu hani naga te kalabus yali pesage tagalama, tama da te
mps	Jerusalemba ma asai, te naga wiegi yai bulu digi dao. Tama nago
mps	bomo dabolo megi ma mobaso, te da bugagia bidibao, da te gasa
mps	hanigo olo sę bidi bidibo tiwai ebadi digi te tagalao wali.
mps	Te Godigo tempel be sunumi tonalubo sę bidi dabego te Israel
mps	hani isąwai we dabe sali bidigo nogi e tiwai, Salum, me Telem,
mps	Tama eno kingba te Asapba te pas me deli asęa mao po hanalu
mps	wai, te bidigo te kingo ni sili elalubo tǫ tonaluai. Te pasgo
mps	agabolo te po waliyu, te pedabo ni nami meba enabolo mao wabo po
mps	pas asęani. Te ni nami dabego te Jerusalem moni masigi obode
mps	sunumi dabe nigiyu, te ami bidi dabego te Godigo tempel be
mps	tonalu bidabo bomai be obo sunumi, te me nigabo ni nami sao po
mps	wabo pas asęai, tama eno be sę yabo ni nami me dao. Tama God
mps	ena dali bidiyu, tama ena tau sai, tama tialima, kingo eno te
mps	hanalu wali nai dabede te usu da po walio.
mps	Tama Baruk, te Sabaigo ogwa, dali te gasa Livai dabego dali te
mps	obo banis sę ebo te Esergo hani sę ebo pąde sę wadolama
mps	yali. Augwaligo bomo eyu, te obo sę ela pali, te polalubo pris
mps	Eliasipgo be sunumi elaluali pąba usu nigi pai dao.
mps	Tama tibaso, eno te sesemone ene me, bainat hwą ge me, enesigi
mps	me, te sę ebo tigidali bidiba dobolama mani. Tama eno te augwa
mps	hani deli deli bage augwa deli kanemeba deliba sisinigi pelama,
mps	bidao po wali. Tama eno augwaliba weyu, te augwali pelama, te
mps	obo banis silisąwani te tigidali badu dolalua peyu, te no
mps	munalu, tama augwaligo te boi bidi dabe dali boi hwįabo sisi
mps	Te Senbalat, me Tobia, me Gesem, me te dago boi bidi mebago te
mps	po odali, te dago te moni masigi obo ma geselebo sę tigidali
mps	silali po odali, tiali goli dago te sunumi musiąbadi dao.
mps	tama te Satu hani bidi te 845 elaluali,
mps	Te Godigo tempel bede musik wabo bidi dabe, augwali te Asap hani
mps	te augwali 148 bidi bidali.
mps	Esrago te bomai po te Hibru pogo nedali, tama te Livai dabego te
mps	Aram pogo begelama, te we bidi dabego bugagia konemainu yai.
mps	Tama te Livai dabego te bomai po page augwaliba pusali.
mps	Nago te naga wiegi yai Mobo Noma Bidi te augwaliba mayu, te
mps	augwali ola momainogo yai. Tama nago te tubo nai mana me wę
mps	augwali menama, te augwali te nai me wę dali tumainu yai.
mps	me Hodia, Bani, me Beninu, te tama dao.
mps	Tiali goli, te meba we bidi hanigo te augwa homu kolesaga wali
mps	pelama, te Jerusalemba bidigi pali, tama te Israel dabego wiegi
mps	yai homu pemene augwaliba yalio.

mps	mebago te musik weyu elabo kapa plet si tola siąo wai, tama

mps	Tama eno te pris Selemia, me te po page koneai bidi Sadok
mps	nigilali, me Pedaia, te Livai hani me deli, te be habu dabe

mps	nigilali, aga nogi te Hanan, te Sakurgo ogwa, tama te wąį

mps	nigilali. Augwaligo te augwa deli sę ebo abagi dabede te nai
mps	dobabo sę ebo kolesaga elalubo dao wali.
mps	Te bidi dabego nogi e dao, Karsena, Setar, Atmata, Tarsis,
mps	Meres, Marsena, Memukan. Augwali te bidi a naga olama, nogo me

mps	tǫ badu te polalubo gavman tobolu bidi dabe dao. Tuni bidigo
mps	te augwaligo po wali paibao.
mps	Augwaligo te po page gegelama, tama augwaligo koneani, te mu po
mps	da wai. Tama tibaso, augwaligo te bidi si te ni pedaide walama,
mps	tama augwali si isali. Nosali king bidigo te po wai, “Te tiali
mps	po te dago dena gavmanigo hasia yali sę po buku, te bukude te
mps	po asęao,” wali. Tialima, augwaligo tama tiwai yalio.
mps	Tama Mordekaigo Estago wali po odama, aga te king bidigo be
mps	sunumi pąde bidali tagalama soali, tama pelama, Estago agabolo
mps	wali po gilama te sę igi palio.
mps	Magi baso meni. Bidi me deligo ena dali, eno hani bage dali
mps	elabo po mia sai elalubao. Agai da tigidali dolabo homu yalio.
mps	Tama timainogo agai te mone maiabo po wai dao. Te augwaligo da
mps	tagala palama, te da kalabus sę iligi sogo da, eno po me wagi
mps	menigi da, magi baso meni, te eno sęgę nagebolo magi
mps	menigio. Tiali goli, augwaligo da mu ela silainu ebaso, tama eno
mps	po hanilibao,” Estago te po wai.
mps	Te gavmango polalubo moni hanu Susade te Juda dabe augwaligo te
mps	bidi sese umabo 500 bidi tigidali ela muani.
mps	Te deli deli Jopgo ogwa dabego, me sogo sogo augwa bede moni nai
mps	mu tuabo sogo bodolu weyu, tama yali. Te ogwa dabe deligo te nai
mps	tuabo sogo bodolu weyu da, aga ama dabe me aga abe dabe tama te
mps	Tama tilama, augwali aga dali tǫba duagulali. Augwali aga dali
mps	bidibadi, nogo a naga olama, me badu nogo badu si sogo aga dali
mps	bidali. Tama augwaligo agade po me wabe, magi baso meni, aga
mps	augwaligo suali, agai tigide moni dene mu saibaso.
mps	teda te be posa pigi menio.
mps	isama, tama megi augwali toma tuyu bidibao
mps	Eno haligade gela naga wabo.
mps	nago homu sęgę genuai mu te eba.
mps	elaluama, sęgę mena tagalobo dao.
mps	God aga dali bidiyu, sę agade ebo.
mps	Ao, augwa wai puluba dabe
mps	augwaligo te nai meni yai bidi dabe dologobeo.
mps	dwagi yai homu elama, bugagia bidaibao.
mps	masigi kemigo sęgę aiyaba ilaibao.
mps	Ena bididuabo page da, mu meni.
mps	augwa kibu kamel dabe teba sela pelama,
mps	Tiali goli, dagego olo ili po naga weyu da.
mps	mani, ena dwai tiwai bidimainu.
mps	Magi baso nago da tigidali sogo
mps	tama da kegebo meni. Mu menima.
mps	1,000 nai dabe hanalu waibao.
mps	teda agai siyu naga ebo dao.
mps	Agai te sę dabe ena tigide ebo digi,
mps	Augwali umagia mu polo pabo dao,
mps	agai Godibolo po weyu, tama Godigo ena eleyu,
mps	Ma, meni wida, magi baso nago ena dąį ilama,
mps	teda eno dwagi yai homu elama,
mps	“Tama nosali da, eno e tǫ tagalama,
mps	te bidi gesabidi poai ame nogobeo.
mps	nage bugagia mu tonaluaibao.
mps	dwai sęge augwaliba me asobeo.
mps	Tiali goli, Godigo homu kolesaga dali,
mps	Augwali olo name ugwa gudubo dao,
mps	sunumi gegeyu, nogogo isisi bilibo tiwai ebo dao.
mps	e tama ola mawaibao, eno dwai sę me ebeo.
mps	Tama nago enaba po wei ponoyu yagameo.
mps	pio ma sasia pabo tiwai dao.
mps	Me sogo genuai wę dali, sigi ge dali si mu
mps	dabe pedalogobe yali ąǫ ebo.
mps	tama nage dwagi yai kolesaga elalubo bidi dao.
mps	“Jop, Godigo homugo nago dene osola sulama,
mps	Te hani augwali augwa bulude bidibo.
mps	Augwaligo homu kolesaga dolo meniama,
mps	Augwaligo dwagi yai nai sabo me usu egobeo.
mps	Dagego enabolo e tama wali,
mps	Godigo ena suyu, godolo isąma,
mps	Eno dwai sę me isąbadi, tiali goli te sęgę dabe eno
mps	meni yai pedelama, tama ena isabo sogo
mps	Tama tigidali bulu badu ena posobo po weyu,
mps	Augwaligo te po wali, ‘Nage moni homu igi.
mps	nago homu kolesaga wali asomaina olama ebawe?
mps	Augwali wi mu ilabo nai dabe da,
mps	Tiali goli, isibo augwaliba asaligo
mps	E sę dabe yali God aga homugo digi yalio,
mps	ena abagi dedego me, ena mu tagalali.
mps	Dagego ena dwai bidibo sulama goli,
mps	“Jop, odao. Nago pogo ena noma selama,
mps	te nai meni yai bidi dabebolo wei ponaibao.
mps	Augwaligo te nai dabe sisinibo si da,
mps	genuai sęgęgo augwali mesegelama,
mps	sese hagala silaibao, te genuai wę asiyu,
mps	Te bidi dabe augwa wai puluba dali
mps	Tama dago ma agaba gedu haluasa po weyu da,
mps	augwaligo augwa we wai puluba
mps	eda soayu ebo bidi dabebolo
mps	Jopgo te aga abagi selabolo te po wai.
mps	tiali goli nago augwalibolo wę mawai menio.
mps	Augwaligo e tama wabo dao, ‘Dwagi yai mu da,
mps	wali peyu, dwagi yai homu elama,
mps	Dagego homugo Godigo bomogo ena aiyaba elaluama,
mps	yali da, tama dego agai homu ma hasegelaibawe?
mps	augwa sipsip dali gea paligi pali.
mps	Augwali bulu du yai madi bidibadi yaide,
mps	augwali dwagi yai homu ebo dao,” wali.
mps	Godigo digi augwali bugagia dua bidimainu elama,
mps	Da te tǫde dwasianu sawi tiwai dao.
mps	nogi weyu, nogo guni sisu, eno mu po naga obao.
mps	“Tama megi da, eno dage ola menama,
mps	Awe, te dwai sę isąwai bagego te dwai bidi dabego silva
mps	te silva dali, gol dali si sainu tibo dao.
mps	Te ba kemodage dabego te bidigo
mps	‘Te dwagi yai homu kolesaga ede me elalubeo,’ po wali.
mps	Tama God da tǫde we bidibolo e tama wai dao,
mps	genuai pesageba sisinigi pelama, po tų odai dao.
mps	dwagi yai kolesaga naga wali pai dao.
mps	Eno po augwaligo haliga tomoba mu pai dao,
mps	eno sipsip kibu dabe me tonalugi pa po wagobeo.
mps	“Tama megi da, te bagego ogwa dabego
mps	Te haniani sę dabe enaba pedelama,
mps	Nago ena te nago tigidali bomogo
mps	eno gesabidi hasegelama, tama husuga sali.
mps	tama kedaugo mu dolobo si da,
mps	tama te polua me ula dwagi yai ebo dao.
mps	teda ena bede ena geme dulaluama,
mps	Eno te eno po meba nage dali pusaibao.
mps	“God Tigidali Bomo Elalubo Bidigo Mobo Bidigo
mps	homu kolesaga dali si edelai dao.
mps	Agai te tonobo da, te olo nai tonobo ąǫ ebo dao,
mps	Tama te bidigo gasa we bidi dali pusuyu,
mps	dwagi yai kolesaga hauwa mu elalubao.
mps	“Tama dage bidi dabe, dagego
mps	bidiyu yaide e tǫ tonaluaibawe?
mps	hulia sai duala sabo madi me elalubeo.
mps	Ma, agai gesabidi dualigi sogo da,
mps	tama agai po sese geda muani dao’ po waibao.
mps	Tama ma, nago doloba pai sę naga idubadi geani da,
mps	agai te bomogo agai homugo yainu
mps	genuai mu yaliwe wabo, tama nago God tagalabo.
mps	tama tulubage gagamainu ebo dao.
mps	Agai te be sele tigidali buluba pelama,
mps	“Jop, nago dwagi yai homu kolesaga mu menio.
mps	eno dąį ilai dao, tama te soabo sunumi paliai dao.
mps	nago te wę pedalobo madi nago suai yali bogo.
mps	e tǫba tudulalumainu ebo dawe?
mps	Godigo Jopbolo te po hanalu wali.
mps	tama augwa wai dabe ena Godiba nai sainu
mps	Tama augwaligo augwalide dwagi yai
mps	Tama augwali udabo sogo da,
mps	Tama hasa digibulu bidibo me tagala,
mps	Tama nago magi baso eno doloba pai
mps	Te hipopotamus augwaligo kau kibugo
mps	Tama dego augwaligo guni pololama,
mps	nago sesemone hauwa mu enaibawe?
mps	Tama te abolo dąų dąų mu olama,
mps	teda augwaligo homu dąų ola selama,
mps	te monu dabego ili nisi tonobo ąǫ ebo dao.
mps	Tama eno te po wali pode ge neyu,
mps	te sogo dolo naga waliyu ebo dao,
mps	“tama me te augwali sigo da kęalubo
mps	Dagego Godide wi elama, tama agade midigi siąo.
mps	nage aselama, ena tau sagasiyu,
mps	te dwai sę ebo kolesaga tagaliąo.
mps	nago te eno gedu haluasa po odobo dao.
mps	God, nago te ena homu dene eyu,
mps	Eno Godiba i weyu, ena tau somainu yali,
mps	te nago augwali dwai dene ilao.
mps	ene dabe sisi yai elalubao.
mps	Te eno nago nogogo nigali dagalu subo sogo,
mps	Tama tibaso, te nage koneani bidi dabego
mps	te bono gągągo augwa digi ma tola sai.
mps	te augwali dolainu ebo da.
mps	tama te dwai sę isąwai bidi dabe asobo tonaluama,
mps	Tama da gasa we bidi dabeba te sęgę me dene mabo,
mps	Te dwai sę ebo bage augwali te tǫde
mps	Te augwaligo dwai sę ebaso, dene somainogo tiwai.
mps	te wiegi yai kapa silva tiwai dao,
mps	sesemane godolo ebo kolesagade
mps	Magi basowe, God aga te agai
mps	dabego nogi ugwaba sabo dao.
mps	Eno dwagi yai homu mu elama,
mps	Genuai Bidi God, nago eno gedu haluasa i
mps	Ena tonaluao, nago naga gedu tonalubo tiwai
mps	tama augwaligo wąį dabe nosali pedalubode me
mps	Eno gedu haluasa po te ena Godiba weyu,
mps	Te magi dwai sę me deli isiąbo te agai koneani,
mps	Te God da, agai kolesaga te wiegi yai mu elama,
mps	Menio. Eno hwįnama, te augwali aiyaba elaluyu yai.
mps	Augwaligo eno po odolama,
mps	Genuai Bidigo ena Devit sa munama,
mps	Tama dagalude Godigo giligago
mps	elalua peyu, mu elalua paibao.
mps	tama nago ena tau siyu, ma dobola sabo bidi dao.
mps	Te agai bomode digi agai ena tau selama,
mps	tama aga genuai nogi mu elalubao.

mps	palama, augwali ela mueibao. Tama eno te ba dabe, me hasa dabe
mps	aselama, te augwali tigi tuagasomainogo yaibao wai dao.

mps	augwaligo eno tempel be pąde mu augwaligo be me ma sę
mps	yagasiyu me egobeo. Polobadu augwaligo be te tama elaluai dao,
mps	tama te king dabe augwali augwa bede isibo sogo augwaligo eno be
mps	meda iliyu yai dao. Tama me augwaligo dwai damua pai kolesaga
mps	eyu, augwaligo eno nogi aiyaba elaluyu yai dao. Tama tibaso, eno
mps	augwali dali sębę elama, tama augwali dolai dao.
mps	Te Sadok dabe augwali naga ena be tomoba asiyu, me eno tebol
mps	pąba asiyu, me eno sę eyu, me eno nai dabe tonalubo sę eyu

mps	hasia wabo poluade nago te gesi kau kibu omai agai tigi kenigo
mps	me dolisąma yai selama, ofa yagasao. Te ofa ebo te eno tempel
mps	be te eno gedude wiegi yai pedelemainu yaibao.

mps	pesage dabeba te we bidigo ofa yabo nai sesebo teba ulugi
mps	dąį iyąo. Te tǫ bobobage te 12 kilomita olama, hap dao.
mps	Tama te tǫ genuai te 2 kilomita olama, hap kilomita dao. Te
mps	da, te we bidi augwaligo tǫ dao, tama te we bidi augwaligo
mps	genuai taun tede nigaibao, te tǫde. Tama augwaligo augwa be te
mps	tǫde sę eyu emainao. Tama me badu bugai te olo tǫ

mps	sulama, te nage wi dwai mu yai.

mps	te Kraisde masigi sisąbo olo sę ebo bidi tiwai pedalama
mps	Te ama mebago te Kraisde konealubo po dąų wabo kolesaga te
mps	bomo me ebeo. Tama dagego te dwai sę augwaliba elama, tama
mps	augwaligo te augwa gedude sę ebo dwai ilibaso da, te
mps	kolesagade te dagego dwai sę te Kraisba digi yaibao.
mps	Tama tigidali augwali te pǫde tamu ąį side baptais sali
mps	tiwai yali, tama te baptais saligo augwali te Moses wali
mps	Tama tiyu, dagego te Juda dabe me, te Grik dabe me homugo
mps	koneao, tama Godigo po odobo we bidi hani dabe me, tama dagego
mps	ebo sęde augwaligo God dali agai po dali si dali dwai homu
mps	idali weyu, dagego duga ebo kolesaga bugagia tonaluao.
mps	Te page delide naga te dage tomode we bidi hauwa augwali tigi
mps	bomo meniama, tama augwali gasi elama, tama augwali meba me
mps	Tialima dage da, da tigidali deliba wadolama, tama dage da te
mps	Kraisgo tigi tiwai dao. Tama dage deli deli te Kraisgo tigigo
mps	haniani sę yabo badu dabe dao.
mps	Tama tibaso, te we bidi dabego konesiąbo pode po wabo bidigo,
mps	agai te po begelabo bomo somainogo eyu tama agai Godibolo te
mps	bomo ena mao po hanalu wao. Tama tiyu, tama agai te bomo sobaso
mps	da, teda agai te aga gasa pogo wabo po begelama, tama gasa we
mps	bidi augwaligo te po page hania koneaibao.
mps	Eno ama dede dabeo, eno wali po page e dao: dagego te Godigo po
mps	pusubo sę emainogo eyu duga homugo bomo elama godolo yao. Tama
mps	me, dagego te da tǫde bidibo we bidigo konesiąbo gasa gasa
mps	pogo te Godigo nogi ugwaba sabo sę te habu munu me selamu dao.
mps	Tama ena dali, te ena dali deli sę ebo bage me, da me sesemane
mps	sogo bidi mebago da dolainogo ebo dao. Te isai bidi ma hodoligi
mps	menigi sogo da, teda magi baso da e tiwai bidaibawe? Te isai we
mps	bidi ma hodoligi menigi sogo da, teda te Godigo pode boi bidi
mps	homu ebo bagego da dene me maidali weyu dago e sę tagaligi da.
mps	silalio! Nage da, isibo kolesaga, te nago dene mabo
mps	Eno homugo te dago Aya God dali, te Genuai Bidi Jisas Krais
mps	daligo, te olo mu da tau siyu mabo wiegi yai kolesagago te
mps	dagego homu nagame ilama bidiąo.
mps	Eno te dago aga sęgę sela sąbo homu yali, tiyu Satango da
mps	tibo po ola menama tama da aiyaba elaluidali weyu tiaibao. Dago
mps	agai te we bidi dolabo dwai homu kolesaga koneai dao.
mps	Te boi bidi dabe augwaligo dwai sę da dali yainogo da pobesa
mps	bilidu gebo dao, tiali goli Godigo da me tagalobeo. Augwaligo da
mps	elama tulaluidu gebo dao, tiali goli da mu me dolobeo.
mps	Magi baso meni. Polobadu Godigo aga we bidi hanibolo te po wai
mps	Dagego da dali dwagi yai homu eyu da godolo mu genuai yao. Magi
mps	baso meni. Dago bidi me delibolo dwai sę me ilibeo. Dage deli
mps	me dolosiąwai. Te dago bidi me deli tibo po ola menama, agai
mps	nai anoma elama me sisąwai.
mps	“Te bidigo te tubo nai nogi mana hauwa sali bidi,
mps	Te dage tomode bidi mebago po kisila ena dali weyu te po wai,
mps	“Pol aga da dali bidiyu, tama aga digi aga aiyaba elaluali,
mps	tiali goli aga digibulu bidibo sogo te agai po bomai asęna
mps	toloyu da dali wabo dao,” te po wali. Tiali goli ena Pol eno
mps	homugo te dagego Kraisgo homu kolesaga hasia bolo kone palao, te
mps	aga digi aga homu aiyaba elaluama tama te bidi dabe augwali dali
mps	nagame yai kolesaga yai, tama eno me te tobage homu eyu,
mps	dagebolo e mobo mabo po megi obao.
mps	Tama dage tede moni midigi me selamuo. Dago koneani, Satango
mps	digi aga tigi hasegelama, tama tigigo naga aga te dwai sę
mps	isąwai wiegi yai ensel mobo bidi tiwai pedalobo dao.
mps	Ena dage tomode bidibadi, te gasa bagego enabolo mani sęgę
mps	tigidali eno bugagia toloyu, tama dage tomode sę hauwa elama,
mps	tama ena da, te Godigo po sela pabo bidi mu da ola mabo bomai
mps	sę eno nogode pedalali. Te e dao: te haniani bidigo isąwai
mps	bomai sę dage tomode pedalali, te Godigo sę sa munama, tama
mps	bidi dodola midigi selama, tama Godigo bomo sumainogo yalio.
mps	Tiali goli, dago digi, ma Godigo sę ebo ensel bidi me deligo
mps	digi te dagebolo dago polobadu wali gesi wiegi yai po
mps	hasegelama, gasa po weyu da, teda da te moni sia dabo buluba
mps	Eno Pitabolo e po me augwaligo gesabidide wai, “Te mu dao, te
mps	gasa hani we dabego da si ame nabeo, te menio. Te Juda hani
mps	isąwai we bidi augwaligo Mosesgo mani bomo yai po konesiąma,
mps	tama augwaligo dwai sę eyu, subigila naga bidibo dao. Tiali
mps	goli da bidi si te Juda bidi hani tomode ame nenama, tama dago
mps	te Mosesgo mani bomo yai po koneai.
mps	Tialima, megi te dena homu Jisasba muabo sogo asaligo da, te da
mps	te bomo yai po dologode bidabo sogo sia sali dao.
mps	Tama te Godigo da dali dąų walali gesi kontrak po, te gesi
mps	pogo te polobadu mani bomo yai po kontrak po aiyaba elalubao.
mps	Eno tede tamadi wali po digi po tiwai po meba te bidi me deligo
mps	Godigo bukude tama po polobadu asęai,
mps	Ama dede, polobadu God agai dage i wai dao, dage olo mu bugagia
mps	bidimainu yai. Tama dage megi olo mu bugagia bidiyu, tama
mps	bugagia suao. Te da te bomo yai po dologode bidisiąbaso, tama
mps	dago polo homu kolesaga wali peyu, tama dena tigigo kolesaga
mps	wali pinao, te homu egimio. Te menio. God agai da tau selama,
mps	tama da olo mu bugagia bidibaso, tama dage duga hasi dwagi yai
mps	homu eyu, duga abagi tau sao, te augwaligo olo sę ebo bidi
mps	Eno ama dedeo, dagede eno homugo dago Genuai Bidi Jisas Krais
mps	agai dage tigidali olo tau sao, te dage bugagia mu bidimainogo
mps	yao. Te mu dao. Te eno po tama dao.
mps	Te God agai dage olo tau selama, tama Satango nogode ma siyu,
mps	tama dagego yabo wiegi yai sę sisi yai. Tama tibaso, dagego
mps	duga polobadu bidali kolesaga ma konea palao. Dage da te Juda
mps	hani isiąwai ame nani we bidi hani dao. Da Juda hani bidi dago
mps	ge hwągo dena tigiwali togobo dao, te da Godigo hani da olama
mps	waselemainogo ebo dao. Tama te Juda hani bidi dabe augwaligo
mps	dage hagede bo olama, “Te God konesiąbaso augwaligo augwa
mps	tigiwali togosiąwani bidi dabe dao,” te po dagede wabo dao.
mps	Tiali goli te tigiwali togobo sę te bidigo nogogo aga tigi
mps	daide naga ebo sę dao, te genuai sę menio.
mps	Te dago Godigo nogi ugwaba mu sinao. Tama agai te wiegi yai
mps	kolesaga ebo bomogo da we bidi tomode genuai sę ebo dao. Te
mps	sę ebo bomogo te da Godibolo hanaluyu gedu haluasa po wabo me,
mps	te dago homude ebo kolesaga te tigidali agai aiyaba elaluyu,
mps	tama agai wiegi yai kolesagade sę ebo te genuai mu ebo dao.
mps	Te God agai dage te gesi noma we bidi nigaligo da, teda dagego
mps	dwai tibo po wabo kolesaga tagalama tama munu me egimio. Te
mps	menio. Tama dage tigidaligo duga hasi tomode mu po naga wao.
mps	Magi baso meni. Dagego koneani, da tigidali te deli tigide naga
mps	Te bidi Krais agai genuai nogi mu elaluama, tama dagego duga
mps	digi aga dologoba muani obaso, duga hasi dali duga ama dede
mps	Ena da te Godigo dwagi yai po pusubo bidi. Tama te tebo pode te
mps	ena kalabuside bidibao. Tama tibaso, ena te wi ebo homu aiyaba
mps	kęna sigulumainu tama ena te bomo elama te Godigo wiegi yai po
mps	pusumainu dagego God hanalu wabo po wao.
mps	Magi baso meni, dage, dagebolo Godigo dwagi yai sę olo elama,
mps	tama agai dage te Kraisgo sę ebo we bidi nigilai dao. Tama
mps	tiyu, agai dage tau selama, tama dagego Kraisde konealubo po
mps	homugo dąų wali. Te me elalubao, te agai dagebolo agai
mps	nogide dene sabo kolesaga me olo manio, te wiegi yai dao.
mps	Magi baso meni, te dagego aga homu wali pabo homu emainogo, te
mps	dagego aga homu wali pabo bomo me elalumainogo, te God aga digi
mps	dage tomode aga sę eyu, tama dagego homu agai hodolobo dao.
mps	Te da Godigo po kibu be hauwa bugagia wali pali bage, te dago
mps	aga homu kolesaga koneai bage, te da tigidaligo te bomo elama
mps	dąį yali digi sabolama, dwagi yai muani nai sainogo uda yabo
mps	homu deli naga yao. Tiali goli dage mebago gasa homu me
mps	elalubaso wida, teda Godigo dagebolo te po page hania waselaibao.
mps	Te God agai dage tau somainogo da sigo gedu haluasa po wabo dao.
mps	Tama weyu, tama sesemane sogo te dago Genuai Bidi Jisas Kraisgo
mps	Aya Godibolo dago dagede puba hwi po wabo dao.
mps	Magi baso meni. Ena dage dali megi bidibo meni goli, eno homugo
mps	dage dali kone palobo dao. Tama dagego Kraisde konealubo po
mps	bugagia dąų olama, tama hani deli naga wadoloyu, tama dage
mps	homu dila pai we bidi bugagia bidibao. Eno dagede tama konebaso,
mps	ena dwagi yai homu pemene ebao.
mps	Duga hasi bidi me deligo “Eno ama dwai sę ena dali yali,”
mps	te po weyu, tama agai te dwai sę ebaso da, te agai nagame homu
mps	eyu aga amago yali dwai sę sęgę sela sąyao. Dago Genuai
mps	Bidi Krais agai dagego sęgę sela sąwai dao. Te tiwai
mps	gilama duga hasi dagego me abagigo sęgę sela sąyao.
mps	Eno homugo Godigo olo tau sabo kolesaga dage dali bidao. Te tama
mps	2-3 Tama te homu elama, da sigo dago ama Timoti dage bidibo
mps	digiba tagala palai. Timoti aga te Godigo sę ebo bidi dao. Aga
mps	te Jisas Kraisde po pusubo bidi dao. Da sigo Timoti dage pageba
mps	tagala palai, tama agai dage bomo mayu, tama dagego Kraisde
mps	konealubo po dąų walomainogo, tama augwaligo dage dene
mps	mobaso da, dage meba bidi te Jisasgo po tagalidali weyu yai. God
mps	aga digi da te dene dali sęgę dali te somainogo, agai da te
mps	Tama te Godigo po wali pisiąwai we bidi augwaligo te po
mps	waibao, “Megi te da bugagia bidabo sogo dao, te da dolabo nai
mps	pąba asogobeo,” te po waibao. Tiali goli, augwaligo te
mps	tobage po obadi, sisi isiąwai, te sogo digi tama augwali
mps	dolabo nai polo augwaliba pedalaibao, augwali noma mu saibao. Te
mps	wede ebo sę tiwai, we mego wai ame nainogo tigide ebo dene
mps	tiwai ebo si pedelaibao, tama te we te dene wi pabo tų menio,
mps	wi sana pogobeo. Tama te tiwai te Genuai Bidi asobo sogode te
mps	Godigo po wali pisiąwai bage augwali wi pabo tų menio.
mps	Tama agai dagego megi te tolobo sęgę sela sąnama, tama
mps	dage da dali olo bidiyu, toma tuabo sogo menama bidaibao. Agai
mps	tebo sogo Genuai Bidi Jisas aga boma pai ensel mobo bidi dabe
mps	dali dagalu tagalama, e tǫba asobo te sogo aga moni sia bogoli
mps	dali e tǫba asaibao, we bidigo bulu ulade hania sueibao, te
mps	Te Genuai Bidi Jisas Krais agai nogigo bomogo dago te tobage
mps	sę ebo bidi dabe augwalibolo po mobo mayu, bomo elama te po
mps	obao, augwali nagame elama, bugagia bidiyu, sę eyu, tama augwa
mps	digi nai sela tumainogo yao.
mps	Agai aga bidibo ulago digi te tagaliyu, te tigidali we bidi ma
mps	abelali. Te tama tiali kolesagade Godigo aga bodolu mani sogo da
mps	ola mani, te agai tigidali we bidi ma sabo homu ebo dao.
mps	Tama po pusubo bidi augwaligo agade po te tigidali
mps	Te augwali tau sabo hani bage meni yai wilawe we elalubaso da,
mps	te Godigo po odobo we bidi hani augwaligo augwa mone gego te
mps	tobage wilawe we tau somainogo eyu, augwaligo nogi te bukude
mps	dago asębo dao. Te bukude nogi elalubo wilawe we dabe naga
mps	augwaligo te tau sabo mone sabo dao. Tama nago te bidi isai we
mps	dabe nogi te bukude olo asęgio. Menio. Te bidi isai we aga
mps	kibu be bidi sese sela wali, te tobage bidi isali we aga bidi
mps	deli naga dali bidali mosi we elalubaso da, teda aga nogi naga
mps	Aga ma asobo sogo te Godigo aga digi sa muani bodolu sogo
mps	elalubo, te sogo te dolo sogo mu naga yaibao. God naga te dwagi
mps	yai homu pemene ebo page bidi, tama agaduba deligo naga tigidali
mps	sę yabo bomo elalubao. Agai te tǫde tuni bidi dabego Tuni
mps	Bidi, tama aga te genuai bidi dabego Genuai Bidi dao.
mps	Te sę dene elama gi bulama tonalubo bidi da, aga te gasa bidi
mps	dabego te gide nai polasa sisąbadi te polasa nai sabo bidi dao.
mps	Timoti, nago te tiwai tama koneao: te tǫ de dagalu si silibo
mps	sogo te pąba yagasobo si te dwai sę ebo bidi dabe augwaligo
mps	dwai sę hauwa ebaso, te Godigo po odobo we bidiba te dwai
mps	sęgo kekainu sinabo sogo pedelaibao.
mps	Te ena ede Rom hanude bidiyu, tama te hasia sogo eno te po
mps	tųde te po wei ponani sogo te bidi me deli ena tau sabo po me
mps	wagasobeo. Menio. Tigidali bidi augwaligo ena tagalali. Eno
mps	homugo te augwaligo te dwai sę te Godigo homu kone me elamuo,
mps	Tama nago agai po ola mabo si te dolo po naga augwali dali wao.
mps	Tama tiyu da, teda nage dali boi bidi homu ebo bage augwaligo da
mps	dali, te nago ola mabo po dali, tede augwaligo dwai po me wabo
mps	usu sąbaso, tama augwali hale yaibao.
mps	Eno dwagi yai ama, Godigo we bidi tigidali nago augwali dali
mps	dwagi yai homu eyu, godolo mu ebo dao. Tama tiyu, nago te
mps	kolesaga eyu, augwaligo homu pua peyu, dwagi yai ilai. Tama te
mps	kolesaga ebode ena dwagi yai homu elama, tama eno moni homu me
mps	esiąyu, te eno homu dwagi yai elama bidibao.
mps	kidu sugunama, tama dagego aga nogi ugwaba
mps	Te nago augwali pedeyu, te bidigo badia pai
mps	Awe, Godigo te tigidali nai bidi dologoba munama elaluai. Tama
mps	agai te nai me deli te olo me augwali dologode elalumainogo me
mps	ebeo. Tiali goli megi dago me susąbadi digi te tigidali nai
mps	bidi dologode elalubeo. Menio.
mps	teda dagego duga olo palia sigio,
mps	Godigo po sela sąyu hagoma yali sogo tiwai.”
mps	Te God aga te dago ebo kolesaga dagalabo bidi bidibaso, dago te
mps	Kraisde homugo konealubo po, te gasa we bidi dabebolo pusabo po,
mps	dago te pode dago homugo mu kęą pao. Magi baso meni, dago
mps	genuai pris tobolu bidi te bidibao, tama aga te dagaluba holama
mps	tama Godigo bidibo digi tomoba mu pai. Aga te bidi Jisas, te
mps	Agai te po bomonama wai, “Eno mu po naga obao, te eno nagebolo
mps	dwagi yai sę yaibao, tama eno nage wąį hani hauwa mu
mps	nosali pedalomainogo ilaibao,” te po wai.
mps	tama tede eno homu me hasegelegobeo,
mps	tama te po wali me pabeo.
mps	Tama te polalubo tobolu pris bidi agaduba deli naga te si wali
mps	be habu tomoba peyu yai. Aga te tigidali kibu bede deli sogo
mps	naga peyu yali. Tama aga olo me pabeo. Menio. Agai te ela muani
mps	omai bulmakau dali te meme dali te sigo kaneme sela peyu te
mps	tomoba pai. Tama te kaneme agai Godibolo ofa mani, te kanemego
mps	aga sęgę bolo sela sąnama, tama te we bidi augwaligo
mps	bugagia konesiąma yali dwai sęgę me te sela sąmainogo
mps	Te ofa dabe augwaligo te kibu tigi sese siago
mps	Tama elalualigo da, teda da homu mu eyu, tama homu si me
mps	esiąyu dago Godiba konealubo po dąų mu olama, tama da aga
mps	pąba pinao. Agai dago yali dwai sę sęgę sela sąnama,
mps	tama dago homu wiegi yai ma ilali. Me agai dago tigi sese te
mps	wiegi yai ąįgo mu telawali.
mps	Te bidi Enokgo konealubo po Godide dąų olama tama agade
mps	tiąlubaso, tama Godigo aga dagaluba sela holai. Aga me isibeo.
mps	Meni. Te bidi dabe augwaligo aga gegebo sę yali, tiali goli
mps	augwaligo aga me subeo. Godigo aga salio. Tama Godigo po bukude
mps	te po wai, “Polobadu Godigo Enok sisąbadi, tama te sogo
mps	Enokgo Godigo homu kolesaga wali paligo da tama tede Godigo
mps	godolo yai,” te bukude te po asęai dao.
mps	Tama augwali tigiba te boi bidi dabego masigi sąyu ela muyu
mps	yai. Tama augwaligo te ni togobo so selama, tama augwali tigi te
mps	sogo togolama pedai pedalai. Tama augwaligo te bobage hwą gego
mps	augwali ela muyu yai. Tama te konealubo po dąų wali we bidi
mps	meba augwali nai meni yai baso, augwaligo te kibu sipsip tigi
mps	waligo me te meme waligo te ugwa tiwai gudama, tama augwali
mps	bilalio. Augwali te tigi tau sabo doado bage tigidali menia
mps	sali, tama te bidi dabego sęgę augwalibolo mayu, tama dwai
mps	kolesaga mu augwalibolo yai dao.
mps	Te ama me deli tula muyu tama Godigo te olo tau siyu mabo
mps	kolesaga tagalidali weyu dagego bugagia tonaluao. Tama tiyu dage
mps	tomode pedalobo ama me deli aga te ha ebo nedu du tiwai walama,
mps	tama dagebolo sęgę menama, tama dage God gedude meda yai
mps	Tama tibaso, da me te pesage nigali te bulu badu agaba pelama,
mps	tama dago agai aga isibode tolali hale tiwai te dago me tolao.
mps	Niwai bidi agai Godigo po ologo naga odama, agai te po wali
mps	pisąma ebo bidi, te aga digi gesabidi te duluade subo bidi
mps	Eno ama dedeo, dage tomode Godigo po ola mabo bidi hauwago te po
mps	ola magio, bidi si sela naga usu yaibao. Dago konebo dao, nosali
mps	Godigo agai we bidi dagalobo sogode, agai da te po ola mabo bidi
mps	dabe agai da bugagia dagalama, osola sueibao. Tama dago dena
mps	sę bugagia esiąyu da, teda agai dabolo sęgę mawaibao.
mps	Tiali goli te sogo agai po odali gasa we bidi te agai dua digi
mps	augwali bugagia dagalama osola sueibao.
mps	Dagebolo magi nai te do pedalabo te dagego konebeo. Tama dagego
mps	bidibo ula te mena tiwai dawe? Te dagego bidibo ula e tiwai
mps	elalubao te kigamu pǫ holama, tama te giliga asobode te po
mps	polo hagabo tiwai, te da bidigo bidibo ula te tiwai osogo naga
mps	Tama God agai dage ma dobola saibao homu eyu, megi dagego Krais
mps	susiąbadi digi dagego duga homu tigidali agaba muyu, tama God
mps	agai dage ma dobola sabo sę eyu bididubao.
mps	Tama dage duga homu tigidali agaba muani bage, te dagego gedude
mps	te aga wiegi yai mu da. Tiali goli te agaba augwaligo homu
mps	musiąwai bage, augwalide te bukude asęani po tama dao,
mps	Te polobadu bidai we dabe sibi augwali te tama tiwai bidai dao.
mps	Augwali dwagi yai homu eyu, God agai augwali dali dwagi yai sę
mps	ebo sogo bugagia tonaluali. Tama tiyu, augwali nagamea pai homu
mps	eyu dua bidabo kolesaga ebadi, augwali deli deli augwa bidi
mps	Tama tiyu aga e tǫde bidibo sogo tigidali agai e tǫde we
mps	bidigo yabo dwai dwai kolesaga munu me egobeo. Te meni. Agai te
mps	Godigo homu naga wali peyu bidaibao.
mps	te nagamea pai homu ebo we bidi dali agai te olo
mps	Magi basowe? Polobadu bidi me deli aga homugo digi te Godigo po
mps	pusubo profet dabego wabo po munu me pedalobeo. Menio. Godigo
mps	Mobo Bidi aga digi te bidi dabe homu hodolobaso, tama augwaligo
mps	te Godigo augwalibolo mani po pusai dao.
mps	Tiali goli, abagi dede dabe mu, dagego homugo te po me deli
mps	gegeda pigio. Te po e dao, te Genuai Bidigo gedude be deli sogo
mps	siade te kibu be hauwa mu 1,000 tiwai te si dao, tama te kibu be
mps	hauwa mu 1,000 wabo kibu be te deli sogo siade tiwai si dao. Te
mps	Genuai Bidigo homude te si te deli tigi tiwai dao.
mps	Dage eno wai dabe, tama Krais aga nogi tobade Godigo dagego dwai
mps	sę yali sęgę sela sąwai dao. Tama eno te po dagebolo
mps	Dago dena ama dabe augwali dali dwagi yai homu eyu godolo ebaso,
mps	tama te dago koneai, dago te genuai sia dabo buluba pabo tų
mps	tagalama, tama da te bidada peyu bidada pabo ula sabo tų
mps	sabolai dao. Gasa we bidi dali dwagi yai homu eyu godolo ebo
mps	kolesaga masiąbo bidi, aga te genuai sia dabo buluba pabo
mps	Bidi me deli agai te po weyu “Eno God dali dwagi yai homu eyu
mps	aga godolo ebo dao,” te po agai weyu, tiali goli te bidi agai
mps	aga ama dali dwai boi bidi homu eyu da, teda te bidi agai tibo
mps	po wabo dao. Magi baso meni. Te bidigo aga gedugo aga ama subo
mps	dao. Tiali goli agai aga dali dwagi yai homu eyu godolo ebo
mps	menio. Tama tibaso, agai te aga gedugo susiąbo God dali mena
mps	tama dwagi yai homu ebo kolesaga egowe? Mu menio, aga usu egobeo.
mps	Bidi mego Kraisgo ola mani po tagalama, tama agai gasa poba
mps	begegi pai, te tobage bidi God te bidi dali bidibo menio. Niwai
mps	bidi me deli agai Kraisgo po dali homu kęą pai bidi, te bidi
mps	te Aya dali aga Ogwa dali augwali si te bidi dali bidibo dao.
mps	Tama te moni tamu ąį bǫį dini wadolama nosali asiyu,
mps	tama te ąį dinigo meda yai pesa hania pedalobo dao, te
mps	ąį sanide. Tama te tiwai te bidi dabe augwaligo te hale
mps	ilibo kolesaga hania ebo dao. Augwali te dagalude elalubo hǫ
mps	meba tiwai dao. Te tobage hǫ osogo ula eyu, ma sula siyu ebo
mps	hǫ dabe dao. Te hǫ pabo te bugagia dolo pabo menio. Tama
mps	Godigo te dwai sisi mu a bulu hulia sai digi sisi yai elalubo,
mps	tama te tibo po ola mabo bidi augwali te hulia sai bulude
mps	sesemane sogo bidada peyu, bidada paibao.
mps	Ena bidibo ula dali bidibao. Polobadu ena isai, tiali goli nago
mps	ena bidibo subao, te ena sesemane sogo bidada peyu, bidada pabo
mps	ula selama, megi bidibo dao. Tama tibaso, eno bomo elalubao, te
mps	isibo kolesaga dali, te isai bidi dabe osogo bidabo madi dali,
mps	te si tonalubo bomo eno elalubo dao.
mps	“Olo elalubo bidi, agai te Godigo Mobo Bidi agai Godigo po
mps	odobo we bidi hani dabebolo wabo po bugagia odao.”
mps	Tama te bidibo ula elalubo hasa me si me si, te augwali deli
mps	deligo bogo te a naga olama me badu nogo deli elaluali. Tama
mps	gedu hauwago augwali tigi te bulu badu me tomo badu me usu nama
mps	mu elaluai. Te bogo dologode me elaluali. Tama ulade dali te
mps	hulide dali augwaligo te balia weyu te po wabo,
mps	haniani tigi yai bidi hanide me, te tigidali genuai
mps	Tama te kibu sipsip waigo te buku dąų wali nai sela wali
mps	togwa sąwai, tama te bidibo ula elalubo nai selago wabo po eno
mps	odali, “Nage asao,” wali. Tama eno ma tonono bilibadi, tama
mps	eno te sisi yai kibu hos asobo suai. Tama te kibude duawali bidi
mps	agai nogode te walu dabe skel ebo nai tolaluai.
mps	Tama te dwasianu sagia sai elalu bidali sogo silama, tama nosali
mps	eno te God gesabidide dolalubo ensel mobo bidi a naga olama me
mps	badu nogo si eno suali, tama augwaligo te ona tiwai nai a naga
mps	olama me badu nogo si selama tolaluai.
mps	Tama tigidali gasa bidi dabe augwali te dwai nai selago ebo
mps	sęde isisąwai bage, augwali homu begelesiąma tama augwa
mps	nogogo nigali nai tagalama tudiba musiąyu me bidaluali. Tama
mps	tiyu augwaligo te dwai haubo noma bidi dabebolo lotu po wabo
mps	tagalobe. Augwaligo te tibo god dabe te kapa golgo dali silva
mps	dali te bras me, te masigi me, te nigo me, tama naigo nigai tibo
mps	god dabebolo augwaligo lotu po wabo tagalobeo. Te nogogo nigali
mps	tibo god augwaligo gedugo sugobeo, ma ologo odogobeo, ma
mps	biligobeo. Tiali goli augwalibolo te bidi dabego lotu po weyu
mps	bidi dao. Nage megi bidibo, tama polobadu mu
mps	Tiali goli augwaligo te webolo te genuai ba kemodage bogo si
mps	mawai, tama te we aga te bidi meni yai buluba bola pabo usu
mps	yali, tama aga te genuai dwai hasamani wi ebaso, aga digibulu
mps	bidigi pabo usu dao. Tama augwaligo aga bugagia tonaluyu nai
mps	mayu yai, tama tede bidibadi kibu be sela olama, polua nogo a
mps	naga olama me badu nogo deli bidaibao.
mps	Te gasa sela wali ensel mobo bidi me te polasa soali ensel bidi
mps	si wali asai. Agai bomonama i weyu, e tama wali, “Te niwai
mps	bidi me deligo te dwai hudigi ebo hasa me, te augwaligo agade
mps	augwa nogogo nigali noma dali lotu po weyu te aga nogode ma te
mps	gesabidide dąį sali bidi,
mps	lotu po nage dali wagasaibao. Magi baso menio,
mps	Tama agai enabolo te po olama, tama agai eno noma bidi te bidi
mps	meni yai tǫba selasa pai. Te tǫde eno te we me deli aga te
mps	mama yai genuai dwai hudigi ebo hasa daide ugwadu dulalubo suai.
mps	Te mama yai dwai hudigi ebo hasa tigide te Godigo nogi posobo po
mps	hauwa asęna pągąnaluai. Tama aga tobolu a naga olama me
mps	badu nogo si elaluai, tama te gąų nogo si me te hasago
mps	yali dao. Tama te tǫde tuni bidi augwaligo me te
mps	Tama tiyu, tama agai dagebolo mani dene dali sęgę
mps	Te masigi hauwa sabo bisnis sę ebo bidi dabe augwaligo te po
mps	waibao, “Te nai nago homu hodaloyu sabo homu yai, te nai
mps	tigidaligo nage tagalama pai dao. Tigidali dwagi dwagi yai tubo
mps	nai dabe te genuai mone naga elaluali, te nago wiegi wiegi yai
mps	tigidali au ebo doado bage dali, te nai tigidaligo nage taga
mps	palio. Tama te bidi dabe augwaligo te tobage nai dabe nagede
mps	munalubo ma sugobeo,” te bisnis sę ebo bagego te po waibao.
mps	Tiali goli agai te dwai hudigi ebo hasa dali, te ili po wabo po
mps	ola mabo bidi dali, augwali si kalabus ilai. Te tibo po wabo
mps	sę ebo bidi agai te bidigo isiąwai bomo yai sę hauwa te
mps	hudigi ebo hasago gedude te sę yai, tama agai te tebo
mps	kolesagade te bidi tibo po ola mayu, augwali te hudigi ebo
mps	hasago dąį augwa tigide selama, te hudigi ebo hasa nomade
mps	lotu po omainogo yai. Te hudigi ebo hasa dali te tibo po ola
mps	mabo bidi augwali si te bidibadi, tama augwaligo te bidi si te
mps	genuai bagua si dedage pageba aiyaba mu sąwai dao. Tama te
mps	dedagede te posolo yai sia dabo masigi salfa elalubao.
mps	Tama te ensel mobo bidi agai ena dali po wali bidi, agai te kapa
mps	golgo nigai dono te hanu usu sabo nai nogogo tolaluai, tama te
mps	usu nigo agai te obo me te obo tų dabe me usu sela sueinogo
mps	E tigidali sęde po pusali bidi megi agai te po obao, “Mu
mps	tama, te ena polo asaibao!”
